***навевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навевать.html>навева́ть</a> (22215)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навеять.html>наве́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navéjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навевать.html>навева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навеять.html>наве́ять</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to blow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навевать.html>навева́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прохлада.html>прохла́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">véter <b>navevájet</b> proxládu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wind blows refreshingly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cast <i>(over)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навевать.html>навева́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоска.html>тоску́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-л</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navevátʹ</b> toskú na kovó-l</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cast a gloom over smb; plunge smb into gloom</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навевать.html>навева́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сон.html>сны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navevátʹ</b> sny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to call up dreams; evoke dreams</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:навеять.html>наве́ять</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>на-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-ве-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ва</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наведение.html>наведе́ние</a> (15143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">навед-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naved-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наверняка.html>наверняка́</a> (1535)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наверняка.html>наверняка́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navernjaká</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>certainly, for sure</li>
<li>safely</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вёрс<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навес.html>наве́с</a> (8105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navésitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hang on, suspend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навес.html>наве́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navés</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навес.html>наве́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навес.html>наве́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навес.html>наве́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>awning, shed, lean-to <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an open-sided structure with a roof</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> overhang</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lob, lobbed ball</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a> (18889)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>ве́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vésitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navésitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hang up, to suspend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navésitʹ</b> dverʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hang a door</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navésitʹ</b> zamok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fix a padlock; fasten a padlock</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to load <i>(with)</i>, to tax <i>(with)</i>, to charge <i>(with)</i>, to saddle <i>(with)</i>, to lumber <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lob
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высоко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голово́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соперник.html>сопе́рника</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navésitʹ</b> mjač vysoko nad golovój sopérnika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lob the ball high above the opponent's head</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>сить</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>на-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-вес-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наводить.html>наводи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to direct <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to aim <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to point <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>след</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navestí</b> na sled</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put on the trail</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navestí</b> na myslʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to suggest an idea <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to somebody</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cover, to coat, to apply

***навешать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навешать.html>наве́шать</a> (27271)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вешать.html>ве́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">véšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешать.html>наве́шать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navéšatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to weigh out <i>(a quantity of)</i></li>
<li>to hang up <i>(a number of)</i>, to suspend <i>(a quantity of)</i></li>
<li>to give it <i>(to)</i>, to give the business, to give the works</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>шать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>на-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-веш-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a> (32286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navésitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешать.html>наве́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navéšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navéšivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навесить.html>наве́сить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешать.html>наве́шать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hang up, to suspend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navéšivatʹ</b> dverʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hang a door</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навешивать.html>наве́шивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ярлык.html>ярлыки́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navéšivatʹ</b> jarlykí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to label; tag</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to load <i>(with)</i>, to tax <i>(with)</i>, to charge <i>(with)</i>, to saddle <i>(with)</i>, to lumber <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lob</li>
<li>to weigh out <i>(a quantity of)</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навешать.html>наве́шать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">navéšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
